(March 17, 2022)</div><div id="a48" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:316.7px;top:354.9px;"><div style="display:inline-block;width:4.5px">&#160;</div>&#8211;&#8211; The Cato Corporation (NYSE: CATO)<div style="display:inline-block;width:5.8px">&#160;</div>today reported a net </div><div id="a52" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:376px;">loss of $6.5 million or ($0.30) per diluted share for the fourth quarter ended January 29, 2022, </div><div id="a54" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:397.2px;">compared to a net loss of $8.3 million or ($0.37) per diluted share for the fourth quarter ended </div><div id="a55" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:418.3px;">January 30, 2021.<div style="display:inline-block;width:4.5px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a56" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;color:#333333;left:185.1px;top:418.3px;">Full-year fiscal 2021 net income was $36.8 million or $1.65 per diluted share </div><div id="a68" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;color:#333333;left:48px;top:439.4px;">compared to a net loss of $47.5 million or ($2.01) per diluted share for 2020.</div><div id="a76" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:476.7px;">Sales for fiscal 2020 were significantly impacted by the closure of our stores for six weeks due to the </div><div id="a77" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:497.8px;">COVID-19 pandemic, beginning March 19, 2020. Due to the impact of the unprecedented closures, </div><div id="a80" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:518.9px;">we will also compare current year results to fiscal 2019 sales, in addition to normal prior year </div><div id="a82" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:540.1px;">comparison.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9px">&#160;</div>Sales for the fourth quarter ended January 29, 2022 were $173.6 million, or an increase </div><div id="a83" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:561.3px;">of 13% from sales of $153.2 million for the fourth quarter ended January 30, 2021.<div style="display:inline-block;width:8.8px">&#160;</div>Compared to the </div><div id="a84" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:582.5px;">same period in 2019, sales decreased 8% from sales of $188.4 million for the quarter ended February </div><div id="a86" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:603.6px;">1, 2020. sales of $816.2 million for the year ended </div><div id="a102" style="position:absolute;font-family:&apos;Arial&apos;;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:704.3px;">February 1, 2020.<div var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
